CC   -!- FUNCTION: Catalyzes the oxidation of various aldopyranoses and
CC       disaccharides on carbon-2 to the corresponding 2-keto sugars
CC       concomitant with the reduction of O(2) to H(2)O(2). Plays an
CC       important role in lignin degradation of wood rot fungi by
CC       supplying the essential cosubstrate H(2)O(2) for the ligninolytic
CC       peroxidases, lignin peroxidase and manganese-dependent peroxidase.
CC       The preferred substrate is D-glucose which is converted to 2-
CC       dehydro-D-glucose, an intermediate of a secondary metabolic
CC       pathway leading to the antibiotic cortalcerone. Acts also on D-
CC       xylose, together with D-glucose the major sugars derived from
CC       wood, on L-sorbose, D-galactose and 1,5-anhydroglucitol, a
CC       diagnostic marker of diabetes mellitus.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: D-glucose + O(2) = 2-dehydro-D-glucose +
CC       H(2)O(2).
CC   -!- COFACTOR:

CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:8319689};

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Catalyzes the oxidation of various aldopyranoses and
CC       disaccharides on carbon-2 to the corresponding 2-keto sugars
CC       concomitant with the reduction of O(2) to H(2)O(2). Plays an
CC       important role in lignin degradation of wood rot fungi by
CC       supplying the essential cosubstrate H(2)O(2) for the ligninolytic
CC       peroxidases, lignin peroxidase and manganese-dependent peroxidase.
CC       The preferred substrate is D-glucose which is converted to 2-
CC       dehydro-D-glucose, an intermediate of a secondary metabolic
CC       pathway leading to the antibiotic cortalcerone. Acts also on D-
CC       xylose, together with D-glucose the major sugars derived from
CC       wood, on L-sorbose, D-galactose and 1,5-anhydroglucitol, a
CC       diagnostic marker of diabetes mellitus.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:8661938, ECO:0000269|Ref.3}.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: D-glucose + O(2) = 2-dehydro-D-glucose +
CC       H(2)O(2).
CC   -!- COFACTOR:
CC       Name=FAD; Xref=ChEBI:CHEBI:57692;
CC         Evidence={ECO:0000269|PubMed:9210340};
CC       Note=Binds 1 FAD covalently per subunit.
CC       {ECO:0000269|PubMed:9210340};
CC   -!- ENZYME REGULATION: Inhibited by HgCl(2).

CC       Kinetic parameters:
CC         KM=83.2 uM for O(2) {ECO:0000269|PubMed:9210340};

CC   -!- FUNCTION: Catalyzes the oxidation of various aldopyranoses and
CC       disaccharides on carbon-2 to the corresponding 2-keto sugars
CC       concomitant with the reduction of O(2) to H(2)O(2). Plays an
CC       important role in lignin degradation of wood rot fungi by
CC       supplying the essential cosubstrate H(2)O(2) for the ligninolytic
CC       peroxidases, lignin peroxidase and manganese-dependent peroxidase.
CC       The preferred substrate is D-glucose which is converted to 2-
CC       dehydro-D-glucose, an intermediate of a secondary metabolic
CC       pathway leading to the antibiotic cortalcerone. Acts also on D-
CC       xylose, together with D-glucose the major sugars derived from
CC       wood, on L-sorbose, D-galactose and 1,5-anhydroglucitol, a
CC       diagnostic marker of diabetes mellitus.
CC   -!- CATALYTIC ACTIVITY: D-glucose + O(2) = 2-dehydro-D-glucose +
CC       H(2)O(2).
CC   -!- COFACTOR:
CC       Name=FAD; Xref=ChEBI:CHEBI:57692; Evidence={ECO:0000250};
CC       Note=Binds 1 FAD covalently per subunit. {ECO:0000250};
CC   -!- BIOPHYSICOCHEMICAL PROPERTIES:
CC       pH dependence:
CC         Optimum pH is 6. Active and stable from pH 3 to 9.
CC         {ECO:0000269|Ref.1};
CC       Temperature dependence:
CC         Optimum temperature is 30-50 degrees Celsius. Active and
CC         thermostable for 30 minutes up to 55 degrees Celsius.
CC         {ECO:0000269|Ref.1};
CC   -!- SUBUNIT: Homotetramer. {ECO:0000250}.
